    (pooler): BertPooler(
      (dense): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=768, bias=True)
      (activation): Tanh()
    )
  )
  (scoring_list): ModuleList(
    (0): Linear(in_features=768, out_features=2, bias=True)
  )
)
